                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-Jabodetabek':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jabodetabek'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-jawabarat':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jawa Barat'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-jawatengah-diy':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jawa Tengah -DIY'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-jawatimur':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jawa Timur'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-kalimantanzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalimantan Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-kalimantanzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalimantan Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sulawesizona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sulawesi Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sulawesizona3':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sulawesi Zona 3'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-papua-maluku':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Papua - Maluku'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-serumaxaonaa':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Serumax Zona A'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-harian':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Harian'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-mingguan':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Mingguan'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-bulanan':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Bulanan'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-ketenganutama':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Ketengan Utama'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-hariansepuasnya':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Harian Sepuasnya'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-zoom':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Zoom'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-roamax':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Roamax'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-gamesmaxbooster':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'GamesMAX Booster'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                                    !i.seller_product_status

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-banten':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Banten'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-naslok':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Naslok'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sukabumibogorbanten':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sukabumi Bogor Banten'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-superseru':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Super Seru'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-cekpaket':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Cek Paket'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-fifaworldcupsmall':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'FIFA World Cup Small'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,

                                    !i.seller_product_status

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-internetsakti':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Internet Sakti'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-roamaxhaji':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'RoaMAX Haji'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-netflix':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Netflix'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-eksklusif':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Eksklusif'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       

case 'telkomsel-flashrevamp':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Flash Revamp'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
